LEFT JOIN [users] AS [u0] ON [u].[user_id] = [u0].[id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[id], [s].[name]
    FROM [status] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[Type] = N'GEN'
) AS [t] ON [u0].[status_id] = [t].[id]
LEFT JOIN [role] AS [r] ON [u0].[role_id] = [r].[id]
WHERE (([u].[branch_id] = @__i_Id_0) AND ([t].[name] = N'AKTIF')) AND ([r].[name] = N'FC')

LEFT JOIN [users] AS [u0] ON [u].[user_id] = [u0].[id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[id], [s].[name]
    FROM [status] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[Type] = N'GEN'
) AS [t] ON [u0].[status_id] = [t].[id]
LEFT JOIN [role] AS [r] ON [u0].[role_id] = [r].[id]
WHERE (([u].[branch_id] = @__i_Id_0) AND ([t].[name] = N'AKTIF')) AND ([r].[name] = N'FC')
